<ol><li>to bury, to dig <i>(into)</i>

<li>to fill up <i>(with earth)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закапывать.html>зака́пывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakápyvatʹ</b> jámu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill up/in a hole</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***закатать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a> (14217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катать.html>ката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукава́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatátʹ</b> rukavá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll up one's sleeves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>ба́нку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatátʹ</b> konsérvnuju bánku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seal/close the lid of a food tin/can; close/seal the lid of a glass jar</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***закатить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a> (10653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll (into, under, etc.), to wheel (into, under, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бо́чку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:погреб.html>по́греб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹ</b> bóčku v pógreb</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll a barrel into the/a cellar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹ</b> glazá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">roll (up) one's eyes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause; to create (a scandal, a scene, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жена́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ла</a></b> андре́ю <a href = vnd.unilang:скандал.html>сканда́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретить.html>встре́тил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аэропорт.html>аэропо́рта</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Žená <b>zakatíla</b> Andréju skandál za to, što on ne vstrétil jejó s aeropórta.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The wife made a scene to Andrey for not meeting her at the airport.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сцена.html>сце́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹ</b> scénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a scene</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:банкет.html>банке́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹ</b> bankét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw a party</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, to deal/mete out <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчину</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹ</b> komú-libo poščóčinu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">give smb a slap in the face</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́ться</a> (14866)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатываться.html>зака́тываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(under)</i>, to roll <i>(behind)</i></li>
<li><i>(celetial body)</i> to set</li>
<li>to wane, to decline
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó sláva <b>zakatílasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his fame has waned</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go off <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>зака́тимся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakátimsja</b> za górod!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">let's have an outing in the country!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go into a fit <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹsja</b> sméxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go (off) into fits of laughter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́чем</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakatítʹsja</b> pláčem (o rebjónke)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into a fit of weeping</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатить.html>закати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>--</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a> (14730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатать.html>заката́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукава́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakátyvatʹ</b> rukavá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roll up one's sleeves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>ба́нку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakátyvatʹ</b> konsérvnuju bánku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seal/close the lid of a food tin/can; close/seal the lid of a glass jar</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>to roll (into, under, etc.), to wheel (into, under, etc.)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ; to cause; to create (a scandal, a scene, etc.)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатываться.html>зака́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakátyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатиться.html>закати́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(under)</i>, to roll <i>(behind)</i></li>
<li><i>(celetial body)</i> to set</li>
<li>to wane, to decline</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go off <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to go into a fit <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатываться.html>зака́тываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakátyvatʹsja</b> sméxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go (off) into fits of laughter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закатываться.html>зака́тываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́чем</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakátyvatʹsja</b> pláčem (o rebjónke)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into a fit of weeping</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закатывать.html>зака́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закачать.html>закача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakačátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зака́чивать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качать.html>кача́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to swing/rock/sway
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закачать.html>закача́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>zakačálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he began to sway; his feet gave way under him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rock to sleep</li>
<li>to pump <i>(into)</i>, to pump in, to inject <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to download</li></ol>

***закидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a> (20217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидать.html>кида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pelt <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> čʹjú-libo mašínu kamnjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt someone's car with stones</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a> кого́-либо (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́внем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́нии</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:осудить.html>осуди́ть</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> kamnjámi kovó-libo (o drévnem nakazánii; osudítʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stone someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> grjázʹju kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sling mud at someone, drag through the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shower <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвета́ми</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> cvetámi (podárkami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower with flowers (presents)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> kovó-libo voprósami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt/bombard someone with questions</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:жалоба.html>жа́лобами</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá <b>zakidáli</b> rabótoj (žálobami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am snowed under with work (complaints)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill <i>(with)</i>, to fill up <i>(with)</i>, to cover <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakidátʹ</b> jámu peskóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill up/cover a hole with sand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ки<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кид-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***закидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a> (16617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заки́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakíd-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to hurl <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баскетбол.html>баскетбо́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> mjač v korzínu (v basketbóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the ball into the basket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> údočku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out a feeler</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> slovéčko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put in a word; throw out a hint, suggest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to toss, to throw, to tilt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> nazád gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to toss/throw/tilt back one's head</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> nógu na nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross one's legs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидать.html>закида́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pelt <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> čʹjú-libo mašínu kamnjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt someone's car with stones</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>камня́ми</a> кого́-либо (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́внем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́нии</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:осудить.html>осуди́ть</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> kamnjámi kovó-libo (o drévnem nakazánii; osudítʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stone someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> grjázʹju kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sling mud at someone, drag through the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shower <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цвета́ми</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рками</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> cvetámi (podárkami)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shower with flowers (presents)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> kovó-libo voprósami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pelt/bombard someone with questions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill <i>(with)</i>, to fill up <i>(with)</i>, to cover <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakídyvatʹ</b> jámu peskóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill up/cover a hole with sand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a> (5618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to hurl <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баскетбол.html>баскетбо́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> mjač v korzínu (v basketbóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the ball into the basket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakínutʹ údočku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out feelers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> slovéčko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put in a word; throw out a hint, suggest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to toss, to throw, to tilt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> nazád gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to toss/throw/ tilt back one's head</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> nógu na nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross one's legs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закипать.html>закипа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakipátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закипеть.html>закипе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to boil, to be on the boil, to simmer, to bubble</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закипать.html>закипа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:закипеть.html>закипе́ть</a>.
